<body class="awsdocs awsui awsui-visual-refresh awsui-polaris-dark-mode" data-new-gr-c-s-check-loaded="14.1270.0" data-gr-ext-installed="" style="display: block;" data-awsui-focus-visible="true"><div id="awsccc-sb-ux-c"><div id="awsccc-sb-a" class=""><div data-id="awsccc-cb" style="display: none;"><div id="awsccc-cb-c" data-id="awsccc-cb-tabstart" class="awsccc-tab-helper" tabindex="-1" role="dialog" aria-labelledby="awsccc-cb-title"><div id="awsccc-cb-content"><div id="awsccc-cb-text-section"><h2 id="awsccc-cb-title">Select your cookie preferences</h2><p id="awsccc-cb-text"><span>We use essential cookies and similar tools that are necessary to provide our site and services. We use performance cookies to collect anonymous statistics, so we can understand how customers use our site and make improvements. Essential cookies cannot be deactivated, but you can choose “Customize” or “Decline” to decline performance cookies. <br><br> If you agree, AWS and approved third parties will also use cookies to provide useful site features, remember your preferences, and display relevant content, including relevant advertising. To accept or decline all non-essential cookies, choose “Accept” or “Decline.” To make more detailed choices, choose “Customize.”</span></p></div><div id="awsccc-cb-actions"><div id="awsccc-cb-buttons"><button tabindex="0" type="submit" data-id="awsccc-cb-btn-accept" aria-label="Accept all cookies" class="awsccc-u-btn awsccc-u-btn-primary"><span>Accept</span></button><button tabindex="0" type="submit" data-id="awsccc-cb-btn-decline" aria-label="Decline - Continue without accepting" class="awsccc-u-btn awsccc-u-btn-secondary"><span>Decline</span></button><button tabindex="0" type="submit" data-id="awsccc-cb-btn-customize" aria-label="Customize cookie preferences" class="awsccc-u-btn awsccc-u-btn-secondary"><span>Customize</span></button></div></div></div></div></div><div id="awsccc-cs" data-id="awsccc-cs" tabindex="0" class="" style="display: none;"><div class="awsccc-u-modal-container "><div class="awsccc-u-modal awsccc-u-modal-large" role="dialog" aria-modal="true" aria-labelledby="awsccc-u-modal-header-awsccc-cs" dir="ltr" data-awsccc-modal-toggle="true" data-id="awsccc-cs-tabtrap" tabindex="-1"><div class="awsccc-u-modal-header"><h2 id="awsccc-u-modal-header-awsccc-cs"><span id="awsccc-cs-title">Customize cookie preferences</span></h2></div><div class="awsccc-u-modal-content"><div class="awsccc-u-cl "><div class="awsccc-u-cl-c"><div id="awsccc-cs-info-container"><span>We use cookies and similar tools (collectively, "cookies") for the following purposes.</span></div></div><div class="awsccc-u-cl-c"><div data-category="essential" class="awsccc-cs-sec-container"><h3 class="awsccc-cs-s-title">Essential</h3><div class="awsccc-cs-s-text"><p class="awsccc-cs-s-paragraph">Essential cookies are necessary to provide our site and services and cannot be deactivated. They are usually set in response to your actions on the site, such as setting your privacy preferences, signing in, or filling in forms. </p></div><div class="awsccc-cs-s-action"></div></div></div><div class="awsccc-u-cl-c"><div data-category="performance" class="awsccc-cs-sec-container"><h3 class="awsccc-cs-s-title">Performance</h3><div class="awsccc-cs-s-text"><p class="awsccc-cs-s-paragraph">Performance cookies provide anonymous statistics about how customers navigate our site so we can improve site experience and performance. Approved third parties may perform analytics on our behalf, but they cannot use the data for their own purposes.</p></div><div class="awsccc-cs-s-action"><div><div class="awsccc-cs-s-cb-outer"><div class="awscc-u-cb-checkbox-container" data-id="awsccc-u-cb-performance-container"><label data-id="awsccc-u-cb-performance-label" class="awsccc-u-cb-label awsccc-u-cb-checkbox-active"><input id="awsccc-u-cb-performance" class="awsccc-u-cb-input" type="checkbox" aria-label="Allow performance category Allowed" checked="true" aria-description="Allow performance category"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="awscc-u-cb-checkbox"><rect class="awscc-u-cb-checkbox-rect" x="0.5" y="0.5" rx="1.5" ry="1.5" width="13" height="13"></rect><polyline class="awscc-u-cb-checkbox-poly-line " points="2.5,7 6,10 11,3"></polyline></svg></label></div></div><span class="awsccc-u-cb-text">Allowed</span></div></div></div></div><div class="awsccc-u-cl-c"><div data-category="functional" class="awsccc-cs-sec-container"><h3 class="awsccc-cs-s-title">Functional</h3><div class="awsccc-cs-s-text"><p class="awsccc-cs-s-paragraph">Functional cookies help us provide useful site features, remember your preferences, and display relevant content. Approved third parties may set these cookies to provide certain site features. If you do not allow these cookies, then some or all of these services may not function properly.</p></div><div class="awsccc-cs-s-action"><div><div class="awsccc-cs-s-cb-outer"><div class="awscc-u-cb-checkbox-container" data-id="awsccc-u-cb-functional-container"><label data-id="awsccc-u-cb-functional-label" class="awsccc-u-cb-label awsccc-u-cb-checkbox-active"><input id="awsccc-u-cb-functional" class="awsccc-u-cb-input" type="checkbox" aria-label="Allow functional category Allowed" checked="true" aria-description="Allow functional category"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="awscc-u-cb-checkbox"><rect class="awscc-u-cb-checkbox-rect" x="0.5" y="0.5" rx="1.5" ry="1.5" width="13" height="13"></rect><polyline class="awscc-u-cb-checkbox-poly-line " points="2.5,7 6,10 11,3"></polyline></svg></label></div></div><span class="awsccc-u-cb-text">Allowed</span></div></div></div></div><div class="awsccc-u-cl-c"><div data-category="advertising" class="awsccc-cs-sec-container"><h3 class="awsccc-cs-s-title">Advertising</h3><div class="awsccc-cs-s-text"><p class="awsccc-cs-s-paragraph">Advertising cookies may be set through our site by us or our advertising partners and help us deliver relevant marketing content. If you do not allow these cookies, you will experience less relevant advertising.</p></div><div class="awsccc-cs-s-action"><div><div class="awsccc-cs-s-cb-outer"><div class="awscc-u-cb-checkbox-container" data-id="awsccc-u-cb-advertising-container"><label data-id="awsccc-u-cb-advertising-label" class="awsccc-u-cb-label awsccc-u-cb-checkbox-active"><input id="awsccc-u-cb-advertising" class="awsccc-u-cb-input" type="checkbox" aria-label="Allow advertising category Allowed" checked="true" aria-description="Allow advertising category"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="awscc-u-cb-checkbox"><rect class="awscc-u-cb-checkbox-rect" x="0.5" y="0.5" rx="1.5" ry="1.5" width="13" height="13"></rect><polyline class="awscc-u-cb-checkbox-poly-line " points="2.5,7 6,10 11,3"></polyline></svg></label></div></div><span class="awsccc-u-cb-text">Allowed</span></div></div></div></div><div class="awsccc-u-cl-c"><div id="awsccc-cs-l-container"><p><span>Blocking some types of cookies may impact your experience of our sites.          Amazon Redshift will no longer support the creation of new Python UDFs starting Patch 198. 
  Existing Python UDFs will continue to function until June 30, 2026. For more information, see the
  <a href="https://aws.amazon.com/blogs/big-data/amazon-redshift-python-user-defined-functions-will-reach-end-of-support-after-june-30-2026/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank"><span>
          blog post
        </span><awsui-icon class="awsdocs-link-icon" name="external"></awsui-icon></a>.
      </p><div data-analytics-alert="info" aria-hidden="false" class="awsui_root_mx3cw_40dx7_215" data-analytics-processed="info"><div class="awsui-context-alert"><div class="awsui_alert_mx3cw_40dx7_193 awsui_type-info_mx3cw_40dx7_429 awsui_icon-size-normal_mx3cw_40dx7_387"><div class="awsui_alert-wrapper_mx3cw_40dx7_299"><div class="awsui_alert-focus-wrapper_mx3cw_40dx7_330" role="group"><div class="awsui_icon_mx3cw_40dx7_368 awsui_text_mx3cw_40dx7_361"><span class="awsui_icon_h11ix_11cyn_189 awsui_size-normal-mapped-height_h11ix_11cyn_248 awsui_size-normal_h11ix_11cyn_244 awsui_variant-normal_h11ix_11cyn_320" role="img" aria-label="Info"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" focusable="false" aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="8" cy="8" r="7"></circle><path d="M8 12V7M8 6V4"></path></svg></span></div><div class="awsui_message_mx3cw_40dx7_371 awsui_text_mx3cw_40dx7_361" id="alert-:r4n:"><div class="awsui_header_17427_1ns0c_5"></div><div class="awsui_header-replacement_mx3cw_40dx7_317 awsui_hidden_mx3cw_40dx7_250"></div><div class="awsui_content_mx3cw_40dx7_391"><div class="fja6OPnQFeFawwoOVDUGnw=="><div><p>
         Amazon Redshift will no longer support the creation of new Python UDFs starting Patch 198. 
  Existing Python UDFs will continue to function until June 30, 2026. For more information, see the
  <a href="https://aws.amazon.com/blogs/big-data/amazon-redshift-python-user-defined-functions-will-reach-end-of-support-after-june-30-2026/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank"><span>
          blog post
        </span><awsui-icon class="awsdocs-link-icon" name="external"><span aria-label="Opens in a new tab"><span class="awsui_icon_h11ix_11cyn_189 awsui_size-normal-mapped-height_h11ix_11cyn_248 awsui_size-normal_h11ix_11cyn_244 awsui_name-external_h11ix_11cyn_355"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" focusable="false" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13 9.012v-6H7M13.02 3 7 9.01M3 5.012v8h8.01" class="stroke-linejoin-round"></path></svg></span></span></awsui-icon></a>.
      </p></div></div></div><div class="awsui_content-replacement_mx3cw_40dx7_392 awsui_hidden_mx3cw_40dx7_250"></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></awsui-alert><div class="awsdocs-page-header-container"><awsdocs-page-header></awsdocs-page-header><awsdocs-filter-selector id="awsdocs-filter-selector"></awsdocs-filter-selector></div><div class="table-container"><div class="table-contents"><table id="w548aac57c11c69b3">
      <tbody><tr>
      <td tabindex="-1"><em><b>
      Client-side encryption for COPY and UNLOAD commands will 
      no longer be open to new customers starting April 30, 2025. 
      If you used client-side encryption with COPY and UNLOAD commands 
      in the 12 months before April 30, 2025, you can continue to use 
      client side encryption with COPY or UNLOAD commands until 
      April 30, 2026. After April 30, 2026, you won't be able to 
      use client-side encryption for COPY and UNLOAD.
      
We recommend that you switch to using server-side encryption 
for COPY and UNLOAD as soon as possible. If you're already using 
server-side encryption for COPY and UNLOAD, there's no change and 
you can continue to use it without altering your queries. 
For more information on encryption for COPY and UNLOAD, 
see the ENCRYPTED parameter below.
  </b></em></td>
      </tr>
    </tbody></table></div></div><p>Loads data into a table from data files or from an Amazon DynamoDB table. The files can be
      located in an Amazon Simple Storage Service (Amazon S3) bucket, an Amazon EMR cluster, or a remote host that is accessed
      using a Secure Shell (SSH) connection.</p><div class="awsdocs-note"><div class="awsdocs-note-title"><awsui-icon name="status-info" variant="link"><span class="awsui_icon_h11ix_11cyn_189 awsui_size-normal-mapped-height_h11ix_11cyn_248 awsui_size-normal_h11ix_11cyn_244 awsui_variant-link_h11ix_11cyn_341"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" focusable="false" aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="8" cy="8" r="7"></circle><path d="M8 12V7M8 6V4"></path></svg></span></awsui-icon><h6>Note</h6></div><div class="awsdocs-note-text"><p>Amazon Redshift Spectrum external tables are read-only. You can't COPY to an external
         table.</p></div></div><p>The COPY command appends the input data as additional rows to the table.</p><p>The maximum size of a single input row from any source is 4 MB.</p><div class="highlights"><h6>Topics</h6><ul><li><p><a href="#r_COPY-permissions">Required permissions</a></p></li><li><p><a href="#r_COPY-syntax">COPY syntax</a></p></li><li><p><a href="#r_COPY-syntax-required-parameters">Required parameters</a></p></li><li><p><a href="#r_COPY-syntax-overview-optional-parameters">Optional parameters</a></p></li><li><p><a href="#r_COPY-using-the-copy-command">Usage notes and additional resources for the COPY command</a></p></li><li><p><a href="#r_COPY-using-the-copy-command-examples">COPY command examples</a></p></li><li><p><a href="./r_COPY-JOB.html">COPY JOB</a></p></li><li><p><a href="./r_COPY-parameters.html">COPY parameter reference</a></p></li><li><p><a href="./r_COPY_usage_notes.html">Usage notes</a></p></li><li><p><a href="./r_COPY_command_examples.html">COPY examples</a></p></li></ul></div>
      <h2 id="r_COPY-permissions">Required permissions<div class="_0RyrTGB0Kc7J6GM+SjQKtA=="><span tabindex="-1" class="_6cXlowEstJU-2JYC67+uHQ=="><span class="awsui_root_xjuzf_1sawi_555"><span class="awsui_trigger_xjuzf_1sawi_590" id=":r45:"><span class="awsui_root_18wu0_3h5y5_934 awsui_box_18wu0_3h5y5_172 awsui_m-right-xxs_18wu0_3h5y5_723 awsui_color-default_18wu0_3h5y5_172 awsui_font-size-default_18wu0_3h5y5_188 awsui_font-weight-default_18wu0_3h5y5_228"><div data-analytics="copyLink" data-analytics-type="eventContext" class="wn3-i0wpB6OIOxt5HoT9uA=="><div data-analytics="r_COPY-permissions" data-analytics-type="eventDetail"><button aria-label="Copy link to the section" title="Copy link to the section" class="awsui_button_vjswe_kruq5_157 awsui_variant-inline-icon_vjswe_kruq5_322 awsui_button-no-text_vjswe_kruq5_601" data-analytics-funnel-value="button:r46:" type="submit" data-analytics-performance-mark="23-1769777759185-7419"><span class="awsui_icon_vjswe_kruq5_630 awsui_icon-left_vjswe_kruq5_630 awsui_icon_h11ix_11cyn_189 awsui_size-normal-mapped-height_h11ix_11cyn_248 awsui_size-normal_h11ix_11cyn_244 awsui_variant-normal_h11ix_11cyn_320"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" focusable="false" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M5 8h6M7 12H5c-2.21 0-4-1.79-4-4s1.79-4 4-4h2M9 12h2c2.21 0 4-1.79 4-4s-1.79-4-4-4H9" class="stroke-linejoin-round"></path></svg></span></button></div></div></span></span></span></span></div></h2>
      <p>To use the COPY command, you must have <a href="./r_GRANT.html#grant-insert">INSERT</a> privilege for the
         Amazon Redshift table.</p>
    
      <h2 id="r_COPY-syntax">COPY syntax<div class="_0RyrTGB0Kc7J6GM+SjQKtA=="><span tabindex="-1" class="_6cXlowEstJU-2JYC67+uHQ=="><span class="awsui_root_xjuzf_1sawi_555"><span class="awsui_trigger_xjuzf_1sawi_590" id=":r48:"><span class="awsui_root_18wu0_3h5y5_934 awsui_box_18wu0_3h5y5_172 awsui_m-right-xxs_18wu0_3h5y5_723 awsui_color-default_18wu0_3h5y5_172 awsui_font-size-default_18wu0_3h5y5_188 awsui_font-weight-default_18wu0_3h5y5_228"><div data-analytics="copyLink" data-analytics-type="eventContext" class="wn3-i0wpB6OIOxt5HoT9uA=="><div data-analytics="r_COPY-syntax" data-analytics-type="eventDetail"><button aria-label="Copy link to the section" title="Copy link to the section" class="awsui_button_vjswe_kruq5_157 awsui_variant-inline-icon_vjswe_kruq5_322 awsui_button-no-text_vjswe_kruq5_601" data-analytics-funnel-value="button:r49:" type="submit" data-analytics-performance-mark="24-1769777759186-3821"><span class="awsui_icon_vjswe_kruq5_630 awsui_icon-left_vjswe_kruq5_630 awsui_icon_h11ix_11cyn_189 awsui_size-normal-mapped-height_h11ix_11cyn_248 awsui_size-normal_h11ix_11cyn_244 awsui_variant-normal_h11ix_11cyn_320"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" focusable="false" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M5 8h6M7 12H5c-2.21 0-4-1.79-4-4s1.79-4 4-4h2M9 12h2c2.21 0 4-1.79 4-4s-1.79-4-4-4H9" class="stroke-linejoin-round"></path></svg></span></button></div></div></span></span></span></span></div></h2>


      <pre class="programlisting"><div class="zKy3ntW31EpIOUhn4g2QBg== BD-nm-vt3Tr2EY8iQBbyIg==" data-testid="codeBtnContainer"><div class="btn-copy-code" title="Copy"><awsui-icon name="copy"></awsui-icon></div><button data-testid="copyCodeBtn" class="_75sMI+SpHdgbiOmB5dQCjg== awsui_button_vjswe_kruq5_157 awsui_variant-normal_vjswe_kruq5_206 awsui_button-no-text_vjswe_kruq5_601" aria-label="Copy COPY table-name 
[ column-list ]
FROM data_source
authorization
[ [ FORMAT ] [ AS ] data_format ] 
[ parameter [ argument ] [, ... ] ]" title="Copy COPY table-name 
[ column-list ]
FROM data_source
authorization
[ [ FORMAT ] [ AS ] data_format ] 
[ parameter [ argument ] [, ... ] ]" data-analytics-funnel-value="button:r4p:" type="submit" data-analytics-performance-mark="29-1769777759190-7709"><span class="awsui_icon_vjswe_kruq5_630 awsui_icon-left_vjswe_kruq5_630 awsui_icon_h11ix_11cyn_189 awsui_size-normal-mapped-height_h11ix_11cyn_248 awsui_size-normal_h11ix_11cyn_244 awsui_variant-normal_h11ix_11cyn_320"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" focusable="false" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15 5H5v10h10V5Z" class="stroke-linejoin-round"></path><path d="M13 1H1v11" class="stroke-linejoin-round"></path></svg></span></button></div><!--DEBUG: cli ()--><code class="nohighlight hljs">COPY <em>table-name</em>

      <p>You can perform a COPY operation with as few as three parameters: a table name, a data
         source, and authorization to access the data. </p>
      <p>Amazon Redshift extends the functionality of the COPY command to enable you to load data in
         several data formats from multiple data sources, control access to load data, manage data
         transformations, and manage the load operation. </p>
      <p>The following sections present the required COPY command parameters, grouping the optional
         parameters by function. They also describe each parameter and explain how various
         options work together. You can go directly to a parameter description by using the
         alphabetical parameter list. </p>
    
         <h2 id="r_COPY-syntax-required-parameters">Required parameters<div class="_0RyrTGB0Kc7J6GM+SjQKtA=="><span tabindex="-1" class="_6cXlowEstJU-2JYC67+uHQ=="><span class="awsui_root_xjuzf_1sawi_555"><span class="awsui_trigger_xjuzf_1sawi_590" id=":r4b:"><span class="awsui_root_18wu0_3h5y5_934 awsui_box_18wu0_3h5y5_172 awsui_m-right-xxs_18wu0_3h5y5_723 awsui_color-default_18wu0_3h5y5_172 awsui_font-size-default_18wu0_3h5y5_188 awsui_font-weight-default_18wu0_3h5y5_228"><div data-analytics="copyLink" data-analytics-type="eventContext" class="wn3-i0wpB6OIOxt5HoT9uA=="><div data-analytics="r_COPY-syntax-required-parameters" data-analytics-type="eventDetail"><button aria-label="Copy link to the section" title="Copy link to the section" class="awsui_button_vjswe_kruq5_157 awsui_variant-inline-icon_vjswe_kruq5_322 awsui_button-no-text_vjswe_kruq5_601" data-analytics-funnel-value="button:r4c:" type="submit" data-analytics-performance-mark="25-1769777759186-4153"><span class="awsui_icon_vjswe_kruq5_630 awsui_icon-left_vjswe_kruq5_630 awsui_icon_h11ix_11cyn_189 awsui_size-normal-mapped-height_h11ix_11cyn_248 awsui_size-normal_h11ix_11cyn_244 awsui_variant-normal_h11ix_11cyn_320"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" focusable="false" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M5 8h6M7 12H5c-2.21 0-4-1.79-4-4s1.79-4 4-4h2M9 12h2c2.21 0 4-1.79 4-4s-1.79-4-4-4H9" class="stroke-linejoin-round"></path></svg></span></button></div></div></span></span></span></span></div></h2>

         <p>The COPY command requires three elements: </p>
         <div class="itemizedlist">
             
             
             
         <ul class="itemizedlist"><li class="listitem">
               <p><a href="#r_COPY-syntax-overview-table-name">Table Name</a></p>
            </li><li class="listitem">
               <p><a href="#r_COPY-syntax-overview-data-source">Data Source</a></p>
            </li><li class="listitem">
               <p><a href="#r_COPY-syntax-overview-credentials">Authorization</a></p>
            </li></ul></div>
         <p>The simplest COPY command uses the following format. </p>
         <pre class="programlisting"><div class="zKy3ntW31EpIOUhn4g2QBg== BD-nm-vt3Tr2EY8iQBbyIg==" data-testid="codeBtnContainer"><div class="btn-copy-code" title="Copy"><awsui-icon name="copy"></awsui-icon></div><button data-testid="copyCodeBtn" class="_75sMI+SpHdgbiOmB5dQCjg== awsui_button_vjswe_kruq5_157 awsui_variant-normal_vjswe_kruq5_206 awsui_button-no-text_vjswe_kruq5_601" aria-label="Copy COPY table-name 
FROM data-source
authorization;" title="Copy COPY table-name 
FROM data-source
authorization;" data-analytics-funnel-value="button:r4r:" type="submit" data-analytics-performance-mark="30-1769777759190-1767"><span class="awsui_icon_vjswe_kruq5_630 awsui_icon-left_vjswe_kruq5_630 awsui_icon_h11ix_11cyn_189 awsui_size-normal-mapped-height_h11ix_11cyn_248 awsui_size-normal_h11ix_11cyn_244 awsui_variant-normal_h11ix_11cyn_320"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" focusable="false" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15 5H5v10h10V5Z" class="stroke-linejoin-round"></path><path d="M13 1H1v11" class="stroke-linejoin-round"></path></svg></span></button></div><!--DEBUG: cli ()--><code class="nohighlight hljs">COPY <em>table-name</em> 
FROM <em>data-source</em>
<em>authorization</em>;</code></pre><div class="programlisting-portal"></div>
         <p>The following example creates a table named CATDEMO, and then loads the table with
            sample data from a data file in Amazon S3 named <code>category_pipe.txt</code>. </p>
         <pre class="programlisting"><div class="zKy3ntW31EpIOUhn4g2QBg== BD-nm-vt3Tr2EY8iQBbyIg==" data-testid="codeBtnContainer"><div class="btn-copy-code" title="Copy"><awsui-icon name="copy"></awsui-icon></div><button data-testid="copyCodeBtn" class="_75sMI+SpHdgbiOmB5dQCjg== awsui_button_vjswe_kruq5_157 awsui_variant-normal_vjswe_kruq5_206 awsui_button-no-text_vjswe_kruq5_601" aria-label="Copy create table catdemo(catid smallint, catgroup varchar(10), catname varchar(10), catdesc varchar(50));" title="Copy create table catdemo(catid smallint, catgroup varchar(10), catname varchar(10), catdesc varchar(50));" data-analytics-funnel-value="button:r4t:" type="submit" data-analytics-performance-mark="31-1769777759190-2807"><span class="awsui_icon_vjswe_kruq5_630 awsui_icon-left_vjswe_kruq5_630 awsui_icon_h11ix_11cyn_189 awsui_size-normal-mapped-height_h11ix_11cyn_248 awsui_size-normal_h11ix_11cyn_244 awsui_variant-normal_h11ix_11cyn_320"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" focusable="false" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15 5H5v10h10V5Z" class="stroke-linejoin-round"></path><path d="M13 1H1v11" class="stroke-linejoin-round"></path></svg></span></button></div><!--DEBUG: cli ()--><code class="hljs sql"><span class="hljs-keyword">create</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">table</span> catdemo(catid <span class="hljs-type">smallint</span>, catgroup <span class="hljs-type">varchar</span>(<span class="hljs-number">10</span>), catname <span class="hljs-type">varchar</span>(<span class="hljs-number">10</span>), catdesc <span class="hljs-type">varchar</span>(<span class="hljs-number">50</span>));</code></pre><div class="programlisting-portal"></div>
         <p>In the following example, the data source for the COPY command is a data file named
               <code>category_pipe.txt</code> in the <code>tickit</code> folder of
            an Amazon S3 bucket named <code>redshift-downloads</code>. The COPY command is
            authorized to access the Amazon S3 bucket through an AWS Identity and Access Management (IAM) role. If your cluster
            has an existing IAM role with permission to access Amazon S3 attached, you can substitute
            your role's Amazon Resource Name (ARN) in the following COPY command and run
            it.</p>
         <pre class="programlisting"><div class="zKy3ntW31EpIOUhn4g2QBg== BD-nm-vt3Tr2EY8iQBbyIg==" data-testid="codeBtnContainer"><div class="btn-copy-code" title="Copy"><awsui-icon name="copy"></awsui-icon></div><button data-testid="copyCodeBtn" class="_75sMI+SpHdgbiOmB5dQCjg== awsui_button_vjswe_kruq5_157 awsui_variant-normal_vjswe_kruq5_206 awsui_button-no-text_vjswe_kruq5_601" aria-label="Copy copy catdemo

region 'us-east-1';</code></pre><div class="programlisting-portal"></div>
         
         <p>For complete instructions on how to use COPY commands to load
            sample data, including instructions for loading data from other AWS regions, see <a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/redshift/latest/gsg/rs-gsg-create-sample-db.html">Load Sample Data from Amazon
               S3</a> in the Amazon Redshift Getting Started Guide.</p>

         <div class="variablelist">
             
             

             
         <dl>
               <dt id="r_COPY-syntax-overview-table-name"><span class="term"><em>table-name</em></span></dt>
               <dd>
                  <p>The name of the target table for the COPY command. The table must already
                     exist in the database. The table can be temporary or persistent. The COPY
                     command appends the new input data to any existing rows in the table.</p>
               </dd>
             
               <dt id="r_COPY-syntax-overview-data-source"><span class="term">FROM <em>data-source</em></span></dt>
               <dd>
                  
                  <p>The location of the source data to be loaded into the target table. A manifest file can be specified with some data sources. </p>
                  <p>The most commonly used data repository is an Amazon S3 bucket. You can also load
                     from data files located in an Amazon EMR cluster, an Amazon EC2 instance, or a remote
                     host that your cluster can access using an SSH connection, or you can load
                     directly from a DynamoDB table. </p>

                  <div class="itemizedlist">
                      
                      
                      
                      
                  <ul class="itemizedlist"><li class="listitem">
                        <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-source-s3.html">COPY from Amazon S3</a></p>
                     </li><li class="listitem">
                        <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-source-emr.html">COPY from Amazon EMR</a>
                        </p>
                     </li><li class="listitem">
                        <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-source-ssh.html">COPY from remote host (SSH)</a></p>
                     </li><li class="listitem">
                        <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-source-dynamodb.html">COPY from Amazon DynamoDB</a></p>
                     </li></ul></div>
               </dd>
             
               <dt id="r_COPY-syntax-overview-credentials"><span class="term">Authorization</span></dt>
               <dd>
                  <p>A clause that indicates the method that your cluster uses for authentication
                     and authorization to access other AWS resources. The COPY command needs
                     authorization to access data in another AWS resource, including in Amazon S3, Amazon EMR,
                     Amazon DynamoDB, and Amazon EC2. You can provide that authorization by referencing an IAM
                     role that is attached to your cluster or by providing the access key ID and
                     secret access key for an IAM user. </p>
                  <div class="itemizedlist">
                      
                      
                      
                  <ul class="itemizedlist"><li class="listitem">
                        <p><a href="./copy-parameters-authorization.html">Authorization parameters</a>
                        </p>
                     </li><li class="listitem">
                        <p><a href="./copy-usage_notes-access-permissions.html#copy-usage_notes-access-role-based">Role-based access
                  control</a>
                        </p>
                     </li><li class="listitem">
                        <p><a href="./copy-usage_notes-access-permissions.html#copy-usage_notes-access-key-based">Key-based access control</a>
                        </p>
                     </li></ul></div>
               </dd>
            </dl></div>

       
         <h2 id="r_COPY-syntax-overview-optional-parameters">Optional parameters<div class="_0RyrTGB0Kc7J6GM+SjQKtA=="><span tabindex="-1" class="_6cXlowEstJU-2JYC67+uHQ=="><span class="awsui_root_xjuzf_1sawi_555"><span class="awsui_trigger_xjuzf_1sawi_590" id=":r4e:"><span class="awsui_root_18wu0_3h5y5_934 awsui_box_18wu0_3h5y5_172 awsui_m-right-xxs_18wu0_3h5y5_723 awsui_color-default_18wu0_3h5y5_172 awsui_font-size-default_18wu0_3h5y5_188 awsui_font-weight-default_18wu0_3h5y5_228"><div data-analytics="copyLink" data-analytics-type="eventContext" class="wn3-i0wpB6OIOxt5HoT9uA=="><div data-analytics="r_COPY-syntax-overview-optional-parameters" data-analytics-type="eventDetail"><button aria-label="Copy link to the section" title="Copy link to the section" class="awsui_button_vjswe_kruq5_157 awsui_variant-inline-icon_vjswe_kruq5_322 awsui_button-no-text_vjswe_kruq5_601" data-analytics-funnel-value="button:r4f:" type="submit" data-analytics-performance-mark="26-1769777759186-7206"><span class="awsui_icon_vjswe_kruq5_630 awsui_icon-left_vjswe_kruq5_630 awsui_icon_h11ix_11cyn_189 awsui_size-normal-mapped-height_h11ix_11cyn_248 awsui_size-normal_h11ix_11cyn_244 awsui_variant-normal_h11ix_11cyn_320"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" focusable="false" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M5 8h6M7 12H5c-2.21 0-4-1.79-4-4s1.79-4 4-4h2M9 12h2c2.21 0 4-1.79 4-4s-1.79-4-4-4H9" class="stroke-linejoin-round"></path></svg></span></button></div></div></span></span></span></span></div></h2>

         <p>You can optionally specify how COPY maps field data to columns in the target table,
            define source data attributes to enable the COPY command to correctly read and parse the
            source data, and manage which operations the COPY command performs during the load
            process. </p>
         <div class="itemizedlist">
             
             
             
             
         <ul class="itemizedlist"><li class="listitem">
               <p><a href="./copy-parameters-column-mapping.html">Column mapping options</a></p>
            </li><li class="listitem">
               <p><a href="#r_COPY-syntax-overview-data-format">Data format parameters</a></p>
            </li><li class="listitem">
               <p><a href="#r_COPY-syntax-overview-data-conversion">Data conversion
                  parameters</a></p>
            </li><li class="listitem">
               <p><a href="#r_COPY-syntax-overview-data-load">Data load operations</a></p>
            </li></ul></div>
          
            <h3 id="r_COPY-syntax-overview-column-mapping">Column mapping</h3>

            <p>By default, COPY inserts field values into the target table's columns in the same
               order as the fields occur in the data files. If the default column order will not
               work, you can specify a column list or use JSONPath expressions to map source data
               fields to the target columns. </p>
            <div class="itemizedlist">
                
                
            <ul class="itemizedlist"><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-column-mapping.html#copy-column-list">Column List</a></p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-column-mapping.html#copy-column-mapping-jsonpaths">JSONPaths File</a></p>
               </li></ul></div>

          
          
            <h3 id="r_COPY-syntax-overview-data-format">Data format parameters</h3>

            <p>You can load data from text files in fixed-width, character-delimited,
               comma-separated values (CSV), or JSON format, or from Avro files.</p>
            <p>By default, the COPY command expects the source data to be in character-delimited
               UTF-8 text files. The default delimiter is a pipe character ( | ). If the source data
               is in another format, use the following parameters to specify the data format.</p>
            
            <div class="itemizedlist">
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                 
               
                                 
            <ul class="itemizedlist"><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-format.html#copy-format">FORMAT</a></p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-format.html#copy-csv">CSV</a></p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-format.html#copy-delimiter">DELIMITER</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-format.html#copy-fixedwidth">FIXEDWIDTH</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-format.html#copy-shapefile">SHAPEFILE</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-format.html#copy-avro">AVRO</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-format.html#copy-json">JSON format for COPY</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-source-s3.html#copy-encrypted">ENCRYPTED</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-file-compression.html#copy-bzip2">BZIP2</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-file-compression.html#copy-gzip">GZIP</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-file-compression.html#copy-lzop">LZOP</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-format.html#copy-parquet">PARQUET</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-format.html#copy-orc">ORC</a>
                  </p>
                </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-file-compression.html#copy-zstd">ZSTD</a>
                  </p>
               </li></ul></div>

          
          
            <h3 id="r_COPY-syntax-overview-data-conversion">Data conversion
                  parameters</h3>

            <p>As it loads the table, COPY attempts to implicitly convert the strings in the
               source data to the data type of the target column. If you need to specify a
               conversion that is different from the default behavior, or if the default conversion
               results in errors, you can manage data conversions by specifying the following
               parameters.</p>
            <div class="itemizedlist">
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
            <ul class="itemizedlist"><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-conversion.html#copy-acceptanydate">ACCEPTANYDATE</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-conversion.html#copy-acceptinvchars">ACCEPTINVCHARS</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-conversion.html#copy-blanksasnull">BLANKSASNULL</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-conversion.html#copy-dateformat">DATEFORMAT</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-conversion.html#copy-emptyasnull">EMPTYASNULL</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-conversion.html#copy-encoding">ENCODING</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-conversion.html#copy-escape">ESCAPE</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-conversion.html#copy-explicit-ids">EXPLICIT_IDS</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-conversion.html#copy-fillrecord">FILLRECORD</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-conversion.html#copy-ignoreblanklines">IGNOREBLANKLINES</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-conversion.html#copy-ignoreheader">IGNOREHEADER</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-conversion.html#copy-null-as">NULL AS</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-conversion.html#copy-removequotes">REMOVEQUOTES</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-conversion.html#copy-roundec">ROUNDEC</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-conversion.html#copy-timeformat">TIMEFORMAT</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-conversion.html#copy-trimblanks">TRIMBLANKS</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-conversion.html#copy-truncatecolumns">TRUNCATECOLUMNS</a>
                  </p>
               </li></ul></div>

          
          
            <h3 id="r_COPY-syntax-overview-data-load">Data load operations</h3>

            <p>Manage the default behavior of the load operation for troubleshooting or to reduce
               load times by specifying the following parameters. </p>
            <div class="itemizedlist">
                
                
                
                
                
                
            <ul class="itemizedlist"><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-load.html#copy-comprows">COMPROWS</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-load.html#copy-compupdate">COMPUPDATE</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-load.html#copy-ignoreallerrors">IGNOREALLERRORS</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-load.html#copy-maxerror">MAXERROR</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-load.html#copy-noload">NOLOAD</a>
                  </p>
               </li><li class="listitem">
                  <p><a href="./copy-parameters-data-load.html#copy-statupdate">STATUPDATE</a>
                  </p>
               </li></ul></div>
